<Review>On May 31st, my nearly 16 year old tabby Lucille started vomiting and acting lethargic.  She's normally a healthy cat, and I don't take her to the vet often because getting her into a cat carrier is usually a nightmare. Kitty does NOT like car rides in enclosed spaces! She had been barely eating for almost a week, refusing the kitty crack that is Fancy feast, and then suddenly she barfed up what little she did eat and then promptly pooped on my rug- something she has NEVER done. My cat has saved my life countless times over the years during terrible bouts of depression, and she's my 'only child ' so I was terrified and sat up with her all night. I called River City the next morning freaking out,  and the receptionist Olivia squeezed Lucy in with Dr. Kennedy same day. I moved to Sac from L.A. 4 years ago, have had cats my whole life, and THIS IS THE NICEST KINDEST VETERINARIAN and staff I've ever taken any of my pets to over the years - the vet tech Jessica was very gentle with Lucy,  the Dr. was empathetic about my not having a ton of money and offered options to help bring costs down,  and she told me Lu was dehydrated, had a heart murmur, and possible kidney issues making her not want to eat. Dr. Kennedy gave her an Rx and a shot of some miracle anti nausea medicine that by the time i got her home,  allowed Lucy to voluntarily eat half a can of tuna and successfully poop in the litterbox again. Yes,  it's that big of a deal! I won't take her anywhere else - when the bill came it was expectedly high, and the staff let me know there might be lower cost clinics i could look for,  but my high drama cat was calm with three staff members, and i could tell she was in good hands.  They are awesome and here's hoping whatever comes back with Lucille's blood work and urinalysis they will be there to help treat. I'm glad i chose them.</Review></record></dataset><record>

< review>
Went here for Dinner last night. For 2 people with drinks included it was around $64+ which is not worth it imo. The Hostess at the register when you first enter is very nice but kept on insisting on leaving tip either while you pay or after you eat. The atmosphere is nice but the food itself in the buffet section was lukewarm and tasted like your average Chinese buffet. To make the long story short, BBQ was not worth it as the meat quality was sub par and the grill didn't get hot enough even though our waiter kept coming back and adjusting it. The Hot Pot is actually pretty good, there was a good amount of broth choices and broth wise it was pretty tasty. They had a decent amount of selections which wasn't that bad at all. I gave this 3 stars because of the BBQ being a bit of a disappointment and how some of the food was borderline bland/mediocre. Would probably only go back for lunch/hotpot since it's cheaper.< /review>

<Rating>5</Rating><review>Very good for Fresno. I've been wondering when Fresno would have a hotpot place, and this place did not disappoint. I've been there 2 times, and I'm definitely recommending it for others to try. They have two sides in the restaurant.  Combo side or the side where you have your own individual hotpot. If you have a large family,  get the Combo where it's enough for a group. Although I haven't been to J Pot, I've heard that it's much better than J Pot. Here, they allow you to choose your own hotpot soup which they have a variety of 8 hotpot styles. You can add any veggies, seafood, and meat of your choice. They have a buffet bar where you can grab your veggies, seafood, and meat, plus other extra food. We had #1 and 8 soup. #1 is spicy and one of their more popular hotpot choice. On top of hot pot, they have a grill on the side for Kbbq. The Kbbq is okay enough to enjoy. They have a variety of kbbq meat to pick from as well. So far, great customer  service. Overall, pretty worth it for Fresno. I would definitely recommend.< /review>< Pictures>

< Text>
This Salvadoran restaurant sits in the middle of Downtown San Fernando. It has 2 entrances. To enter the front you would have to park in the metered spots. If you want to go in the rear entrance there is plenty of city and street parking for free.
The server Veronica is super nice and extremely accommodating to the clientele. I had Pupusas that were good and the price from Monday-Friday are $1.25 each. Unlike other places that includes all of their selections. Most of the menu is traditional Salvadoran with a splash of Mexican dishes.<//Text>

Located in a run down area, but worth the quick drive from Valley Fair Mall, and once inside, a feast awaits you. Large booths, private party room. This restaurant has been around for a long time, once a palace feel, now some of the vinyl on the booths reveals its age and wear. Bulgogi is sweet and tender and addictive! A good deal on lunch. Quality food and freshly made typical Korean dishes. Overseen by the owners who are usually there, and same waiters and waitresses who do not seem to age. Recent visit revealed new seat cushions! < Review>
The decor and sign may be dated, but this is some of the most reliably good Korean food in town. Try the table grilled meats, the stone pot specialties and enjoy endlessly replenished sides of vegetables,  kimchee, tofu and other yummy things. No frills, just good comfort food.</Review>

< Text>
The quality of the food is good and the staff are  very friendly. The reason I would not give this place 5 stars is because of the amount of food given and the fam that that there are only certain items on the menu that allow you to use the table top grill. Also, it is quite pricey for the amount. My wife and I paid $60 for a combination plate that comes with 4 types of meats. Most Korean BBQ places have a flat rate and it's all you can eat....not here. All in all, it is a nice little restaurant but I will no be frequenting it.</Text>

An old Korean restaurant has to compete with newer ones so if you can't beat fresh new fusion by price, decor, or service then you'll be in trouble.

The problem with this is the event is run inefficient and poorly.  Normally places charge by the person but here they charge by plate used. Really odd considering guest don't know that so some guest grab two plates or a new plate for seconds.

DIY. Bad business practice and skimps on meats for events.</Review>
